<Rate>5< /Rate>< Review>
Stumbled upon this place as I was shopping at Walgreens across the (mini) lot.  From the outside, looking in, you could see the simple, clean layout of the office.  From setting up an appointment online, to filling out the online forms, to taking your first steps into the office, everything is so organized and well laid out.

I love the black and white theme and (I know, i know... it's clean and new now) everything is just so pleasant and easy on the eyes.  This adds to feeling more at ease while at the dreaded dental office.  On top of that, there's a TV in front, and on top of you, for when you're in either the upright or reclined position.  You can just Netflix and Chill (not that kind of chill...) while Dr. Kim operates on your teeth.  You'll be equipped with protective eye-wear and a set of wireless headphones to distract you from the drilling and grinding of your teeth.

Another plus here is that all your documents are on their tablet so instead of pretending to read everything, they can just watch me swipe down to the bottom and sign my life away.  On that same tablet, I do like how all of his findings from my scans are listed out and prioritized for which "issues" to address first.  What's also great is that your insurance/out-of-pocket costs are all presented in front of you so that you can see when your insurance coverage for the year has been exhausted.  Instead of cheaping out and "risking it" to save a few bucks on the extensive number of items my teeth need attending to, Dr. Kim will let you know what he thinks are major concerns that should be addressed as soon as possible, and then the items you can defer to next year when your insurance will cover some more.

If only i brushed twice a day AND flossed more routinely...  oh well...  YOLO!

TL;DR - if you haven't been to a dentist in a while, you might as well start now.  I fully recommend Dr. Kim to be your next dentist you see on the regular.  Shout out to his assistants as well!  They make everything pleasant while visiting the dentist.

oh yeah...i got a nice care package during my first visit!  It's a nice touch.

+1 oh yeah...  my temp crown fell out and notified Dr. Kim around noon and his office got back to me and scheduled me for a 4:30pm appointment to get me back on my chewing ways...  great service!</Review>

<pictures>None< /pictures><text>Stumbled upon this place as I was shopping at Walgreens across the (mini) lot.  From the outside, looking in, you could see the simple, clean layout of the office.  From setting up an appointment online, to filling out the online forms, to taking your first steps into the office, everything is so organized and well laid out.

I love the black and white theme and (I know, i know... it's clean and new now) everything is just so pleasant and easy on the eyes.  This adds to feeling more at ease while at the dreaded dental office.  On top of that, there's a TV in front, and on top of you, for when you're in either the upright or reclined position.  You can just Netflix and Chill (not that kind of chill...) while Dr. Kim operates on your teeth.  You'll be equipped with protective eye-wear and a set of wireless headphones to distract you from the drilling and grinding of your teeth.

Another plus here is that all your documents are on their tablet so instead of pretending to read everything, they can just watch me swipe down to the bottom and sign my life away.  On that same tablet, I do like how all of his findings from my scans are listed out and prioritized for which "issues" to address first.  What's also great is that your insurance/out-of-pocket costs are all presented in front of you so that you can see when your insurance coverage for the year has been exhausted.  Instead of cheaping out and "risking it" to save a few bucks on the extensive number of items my teeth need attending to, Dr. Kim will let you know what he thinks are major concerns that should be addressed as soon as possible, and then the items you can defer to next year when your insurance will cover some more.

If only i brushed twice a day AND flossed more routinely...  oh well...  YOLO!

TL;DR - if you haven't been to a dentist in a while, you might as well start now.  I fully recommend Dr. Kim to be your next dentist you see on the regular.  Shout out to his assistants as well!  They make everything pleasant while visiting the dentist.

oh yeah...i got a nice care package during my first visit!  It's a nice touch.

This place was really good.  What made this a 4 and not a 5 was the service, everyone was nice and good customer service, just the process from ordering to paying took a long time (will call ahead next time). The food was excellent and fresh. The price was up there but you got what you paid for. The next day we ate our leftovers, though it was microwaved it heated well. Did I mention the sides are ginormous? We will be back for sure!<//Review>

<text>Went to this barbecue place last year but it was closed.  Went back yesterday and picked up a rack of pork ribs.  Also a small side of sweet potatos with walnuts/pecans (I forgot which).

The ribs were outstanding.  The meat was so tender it had me sucking on the bone!  You can tell the quality of barbequed meat by the way it taste without all the sauces and condiments.  These ribs needed no additional sauce or anything to enhance their smoked flavor.  Although I did use a little of the sauce provided on the side, it was tangy and sweet at the same time.  Most importantly,, it doesn't overpower the meat.  A little bit goes a long way.

The sweet potatoes were tasty as well and complimented the ribs very well. The only thing about this dish was that were a bit too many walnuts/pecans for my taste.  Never the less, I will be returning soon to try their brisket and other offerings.<//text>< Response>

<time>1620366425731</time><rating>5<//rating>< text>
I admit the owner is my long time friend. But I am also a critic of food and brutally honest.
Ricky Hernandez studies and masters whatever he does to the finest detail.
The meat is cooked to perfection and is moist and flavorful. The bbq sauce is well balanced with a smokey flavor. The Mac and cheese made with smoked gouda.
Backed beans not too sweet with bits of "burnt ends" from the brisket in them.
Sweet potatoes just right with pecans and well balanced.
Cured pickels made the real way.
Pickled onions to refresh the pallet.
I wish the coleslaw had more vinegar ( just my preference) although it is very fresh tasting.
Gourmet beverages from Sprecher craft sodas, kombucha and mineral water in glass bottles.
A Very enjoyable experience.

Just ate a leftover piece of brisket from the fridge, still moist and the flavor is excellent cold.
Real meat eaters will understand.< /text>

<user>111008602933755792887< /user>< Text>
Finally got time to try Jude‚Äôs BBQ. First thing I noticed - wonderful smoke smell inside the place. Second, the owner works the counter, slicing brisket.  Ordered two brisket sandwiches. He asks, ‚ÄúFatty or Lean?‚Äù (never had a bbq place ask that if me before).  I said his choice, so he gave us a bit of both. Toasted buns. You can get them topped with sauce, pickles, slaw or pickled red onions.  We ordered slaw and beans as sides.

Verdict: Yum!  Some of the best brisket i‚Äôve had in a very long time.  No dry spots, not tough, not overly fat, nice crust & smoke ring. Slaw tasted homemade, beans were loaded with meat & flavor. Sauce is nice, not too ketchupy or sweet, but no burn.

Also available were spareribs, pulled pork, sausage and (today) beef short ribs.

Everybody was masked & gloved up. Hand sanitizer is available on a table.

He said they run out early and close when they do, so come early.

Definitely, Definitely will be back!!</Text>

Really great Mexican place! You get exactly what you would expect from any other taqueria. I do really love the 2-meat option burrito because it's fun to mix'n'match and not be limited to one meat choice, even though I got 2 types of pork. What can I say, pork is amazing.

<rate>4< /rate>< review>
If you want some SoCal authentic Mexican food and you want it cheap then go here. Their portions are huge and their meat is greasy, but their veggies may or may not be the freshest around. The burritos and quesadillas seem to be the most popular items, both being oversized and absolutely stuffed with meat. Both the beef and chicken are tasty, I haven't ventured into the beef tongue yet! Don't expect a huge variety here though, they pretty much just have a couple salsas, cheese, onions and cilantro.<//review>
